##### **Scalable High-Recall Constraint-Satisfaction-Based Information Retrieval for Clinical Trials Matching**
2604.08849v1 by Cyrus Zhou, Yufei Jin, Yilin Xu, Yu-Chiang Wang, Chieh-Ju Chao, Monica S. Lam

Clinical trials are central to evidence-based medicine, yet many struggle to meet enrollment targets, despite the availability of over half a million trials listed on ClinicalTrials.gov, which attracts approximately two million users monthly. Existing retrieval techniques, largely based on keyword and embedding-similarity matching between patient profiles and eligibility criteria, often struggle with low recall, low precision, and limited interpretability due to complex constraints. We propose SatIR, a scalable clinical trial retrieval method based on constraint satisfaction, enabling high-precision and interpretable matching of patients to relevant trials. Our approach uses formal methods -- Satisfiability Modulo Theories (SMT) and relational algebra -- to efficiently represent and match key constraints from clinical trials and patient records. Beyond leveraging established medical ontologies and conceptual models, we use Large Language Models (LLMs) to convert informal reasoning regarding ambiguity, implicit clinical assumptions, and incomplete patient records into explicit, precise, controllable, and interpretable formal constraints. Evaluated on 59 patients and 3,621 trials, SatIR outperforms TrialGPT on all three evaluated retrieval objectives. It retrieves 32%-72% more relevant-and-eligible trials per patient, improves recall over the union of useful trials by 22-38 points, and serves more patients with at least one useful trial. Retrieval is fast, requiring 2.95 seconds per patient over 3,621 trials. These results show that SatIR is scalable, effective, and interpretable.

摘要：臨床試驗是循證醫學的核心，但儘管 ClinicalTrials.gov 上列出了超過五十萬個試驗，每月吸引約兩百萬用戶，許多試驗仍然難以達到招募目標。現有的檢索技術主要基於關鍵字和患者檔案與資格標準之間的嵌入相似度匹配，往往面臨低召回率、低精確度和由於複雜約束導致的有限可解釋性問題。我們提出了 SatIR，一種基於約束滿足的可擴展臨床試驗檢索方法，能夠高精度和可解釋地將患者與相關試驗匹配。我們的方法使用形式化方法——滿足性模組理論（SMT）和關係代數——來有效地表示和匹配臨床試驗和患者記錄中的關鍵約束。除了利用既有的醫學本體論和概念模型外，我們還使用大型語言模型（LLMs）將有關模糊性、隱含臨床假設和不完整患者記錄的非正式推理轉換為明確、精確、可控和可解釋的形式約束。在對59名患者和3,621個試驗進行評估後，SatIR 在所有三個評估的檢索目標上均優於 TrialGPT。它每位患者檢索到的相關且符合資格的試驗多出32%-72%，在有用試驗的聯集上提高了22-38個點的召回率，並為更多患者提供至少一個有用的試驗。檢索速度快，對每位患者在3,621個試驗中僅需2.95秒。這些結果表明，SatIR 是可擴展的、有效的和可解釋的。

##### **STaR-DRO: Stateful Tsallis Reweighting for Group-Robust Structured Prediction**
2604.09737v1 by Samah Fodeh, Ganesh Puthiaraju, Elyas Irankhah, Linhai Ma, Srivani Talakokkul, Afshan Khan, Sreeraj Ramachandran, Jordan Alpert, Sarah Schellhorn

Structured prediction requires models to generate ontology-constrained labels, grounded evidence, and valid structure under ambiguity, label skew, and heterogeneous group difficulty. We present a two-part framework for controllable inference and robust fine-tuning. First, we introduce a task-agnostic prompting strategy that combines XML-based instruction structure, disambiguation rules, verification-style reasoning, schema constraints, and self-validation to address format drift, label ambiguity, evidence hallucination, and metadata-conditioned confusion in in-context structured generation. Second, we introduce STaR-DRO, a stateful robust optimization method for group heterogeneity. It combines Tsallis mirror descent with momentum-smoothed, centered group-loss signals and bounded excess-only multipliers so that only persistently hard groups above a neutral baseline are upweighted, concentrating learning where it is most needed while avoiding volatile, dense exponentiated-gradient reweighting and unnecessary loss from downweighting easier groups. We evaluate the combined framework on EPPC Miner, a benchmark for extracting hierarchical labels and evidence spans from patient-provider secure messages. Prompt engineering improves zero-shot by +15.44 average F1 across Code, Sub-code, and Span over four Llama models. Building on supervised fine-tuning, STaR-DRO further improves the hardest semantic decisions: on Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct, Code F1 rises from 79.24 to 81.47 and Sub-code F1 from 67.78 to 69.30, while preserving Span performance and reducing group-wise validation cross-entropy by up to 29.6% on the most difficult clinical categories. Because these rare and difficult groups correspond to clinically consequential communication behaviors, these gains are not merely statistical improvements: they directly strengthen communication mining reliability for patient-centered care analysis.

摘要：結構化預測要求模型在模糊性、標籤偏差和異質性群體困難下生成受本體約束的標籤、基於證據的內容和有效結構。我們提出了一個由兩部分組成的框架，用於可控推理和穩健的微調。首先，我們介紹了一種與任務無關的提示策略，該策略結合了基於XML的指令結構、消歧規則、驗證式推理、模式約束和自我驗證，以解決上下文結構生成中的格式漂移、標籤模糊、證據幻覺和元數據條件混淆。其次，我們介紹了STaR-DRO，一種針對群體異質性的有狀態穩健優化方法。它結合了Tsallis鏡像下降與動量平滑的集中群體損失信號和有界的超額乘子，這樣只有持續困難的群體在中性基準之上被加權，提高學習集中在最需要的地方，同時避免不穩定的、密集的指數梯度重加權和因降低較易群體權重而產生的不必要損失。我們在EPPC Miner上評估了這個綜合框架，該基準用於從患者與提供者的安全消息中提取層次標籤和證據範圍。提示工程使得零樣本的平均F1在四個Llama模型上提高了+15.44，涵蓋了代碼、子代碼和範圍。在監督微調的基礎上，STaR-DRO進一步改善了最困難的語義決策：在Llama-3.3-70B-Instruct上，代碼F1從79.24上升到81.47，子代碼F1從67.78上升到69.30，同時保持範圍性能並將最困難臨床類別的群體驗證交叉熵降低了多達29.6%。因為這些稀有且困難的群體與臨床上重要的溝通行為相對應，這些增益不僅僅是統計上的改善：它們直接增強了以患者為中心的護理分析中的溝通挖掘可靠性。

##### **Quantifying Explanation Consistency: The C-Score Metric for CAM-Based Explainability in Medical Image Classification**
2604.08502v1 by Kabilan Elangovan, Daniel Ting

Class Activation Mapping (CAM) methods are widely used to generate visual explanations for deep learning classifiers in medical imaging. However, existing evaluation frameworks assess whether explanations are correct, measured by localisation fidelity against radiologist annotations, rather than whether they are consistent: whether the model applies the same spatial reasoning strategy across different patients with the same pathology. We propose the C-Score (Consistency Score), a confidence-weighted, annotation-free metric that quantifies intra-class explanation reproducibility via intensity-emphasised pairwise soft IoU across correctly classified instances. We evaluate six CAM techniques: GradCAM, GradCAM++, LayerCAM, EigenCAM, ScoreCAM, and MS GradCAM++ across three CNN architectures (DenseNet201, InceptionV3, ResNet50V2) over thirty training epochs on the Kermany chest X-ray dataset, covering transfer learning and fine-tuning phases. We identify three distinct mechanisms of AUC-consistency dissociation, invisible to standard classification metrics: threshold-mediated gold list collapse, technique-specific attribution collapse at peak AUC, and class-level consistency masking in global aggregation. C-Score provides an early warning signal of impending model instability. ScoreCAM deterioration on ResNet50V2 is detectable one full checkpoint before catastrophic AUC collapse and yields architecture-specific clinical deployment recommendations grounded in explanation quality rather than predictive ranking alone.

摘要：類別激活映射（CAM）方法被廣泛用於生成醫學影像中深度學習分類器的視覺解釋。<lb/>然而，現有的評估框架評估解釋是否正確，通過與放射科醫生註釋的定位忠實度來衡量，而不是評估它們是否一致：即模型是否在具有相同病理的不同患者之間應用相同的空間推理策略。<lb/>我們提出了C-Score（一致性分數），這是一種基於信心加權的無註釋指標，通過強調強度的成對軟IoU量化類內解釋的可重複性，針對正確分類的實例。<lb/>我們在Kermany胸部X光數據集上評估六種CAM技術：GradCAM、GradCAM++、LayerCAM、EigenCAM、ScoreCAM和MS GradCAM++，涵蓋三種CNN架構（DenseNet201、InceptionV3、ResNet50V2），並在三十個訓練週期內進行轉移學習和微調階段的評估。<lb/>我們識別出三種AUC一致性解離的不同機制，這些機制對標準分類指標來說是不可見的：閾值介導的金名單崩潰、在峰值AUC時的技術特定歸因崩潰，以及在全局聚合中的類別級一致性掩蔽。<lb/>C-Score提供了即將發生的模型不穩定性的早期警告信號。<lb/>在ResNet50V2上，ScoreCAM的惡化在災難性AUC崩潰之前可以檢測到一個完整的檢查點，並基於解釋質量而非僅僅是預測排名，提供架構特定的臨床部署建議。

##### **A Machine Learning Framework for Turbofan Health Estimation via Inverse Problem Formulation**
2604.08460v1 by Milad Leyli-Abadi, Lucas Thil, Sebastien Razakarivony, Guillaume Doquet, Jesse Read

Estimating the health state of turbofan engines is a challenging ill-posed inverse problem, hindered by sparse sensing and complex nonlinear thermodynamics. Research in this area remains fragmented, with comparisons limited by the use of unrealistic datasets and insufficient exploration of the exploitation of temporal information. This work investigates how to recover component-level health indicators from operational sensor data under realistic degradation and maintenance patterns. To support this study, we introduce a new dataset that incorporates industry-oriented complexities such as maintenance events and usage changes. Using this dataset, we establish an initial benchmark that compares steady-state and nonstationary data-driven models, and Bayesian filters, classic families of methods used to solve this problem. In addition to this benchmark, we introduce self-supervised learning (SSL) approaches that learn latent representations without access to true health labels, a scenario reflective of real-world operational constraints. By comparing the downstream estimation performance of these unsupervised representations against the direct prediction baselines, we establish a practical lower bound on the difficulty of solving this inverse problem. Our results reveal that traditional filters remain strong baselines, while SSL methods reveal the intrinsic complexity of health estimation and highlight the need for more advanced and interpretable inference strategies. For reproducibility, both the generated dataset and the implementation used in this work are made accessible.

摘要：估計渦扇發動機的健康狀態是一個具有挑戰性的病態反問題，受到稀疏感測和複雜非線性熱力學的阻礙。這個領域的研究仍然是支離破碎的，因為比較受到不現實數據集的限制，以及對時間信息利用的探索不足。這項工作研究如何在現實的退化和維護模式下，從操作傳感器數據中恢復組件級健康指標。為了支持這項研究，我們引入了一個新的數據集，該數據集考慮了行業導向的複雜性，例如維護事件和使用變化。利用這個數據集，我們建立了一個初步基準，對比穩態和非穩態數據驅動模型，以及貝葉斯濾波器，這些都是用來解決這個問題的經典方法家族。除了這個基準，我們還引入了自我監督學習（SSL）方法，這些方法在沒有真實健康標籤的情況下學習潛在表示，這是一種反映現實操作約束的情境。通過將這些無監督表示的下游估計性能與直接預測基準進行比較，我們確立了解決這個反問題的難度的實際下限。我們的結果顯示，傳統濾波器仍然是強有力的基準，而SSL方法揭示了健康估計的內在複雜性，並強調了對更先進和可解釋的推斷策略的需求。為了可重複性，這項工作中生成的數據集和實施方法都已公開。

##### **Lost in the Hype: Revealing and Dissecting the Performance Degradation of Medical Multimodal Large Language Models in Image Classification**
2604.08333v1 by Xun Zhu, Fanbin Mo, Xi Chen, Kaili Zheng, Shaoshuai Yang, Yiming Shi, Jian Gao, Miao Li, Ji Wu

The rise of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) has sparked an unprecedented wave of applications in the field of medical imaging analysis. However, as one of the earliest and most fundamental tasks integrated into this paradigm, medical image classification reveals a sobering reality: state-of-the-art medical MLLMs consistently underperform compared to traditional deep learning models, despite their overwhelming advantages in pre-training data and model parameters. This paradox prompts a critical rethinking: where exactly does the performance degradation originate? In this paper, we conduct extensive experiments on 14 open-source medical MLLMs across three representative image classification datasets. Moving beyond superficial performance benchmarking, we employ feature probing to track the information flow of visual features module-by-module and layer-by-layer throughout the entire MLLM pipeline, enabling explicit visualization of where and how classification signals are distorted, diluted, or overridden. As the first attempt to dissect classification performance degradation in medical MLLMs, our findings reveal four failure modes: 1) quality limitation in visual representation, 2) fidelity loss in connector projection, 3) comprehension deficit in LLM reasoning, and 4) misalignment of semantic mapping. Meanwhile, we introduce quantitative scores that characterize the healthiness of feature evolution, enabling principled comparisons across diverse MLLMs and datasets. Furthermore, we provide insightful discussions centered on the critical barriers that prevent current medical MLLMs from fulfilling their promised clinical potential. We hope that our work provokes rethinking within the community-highlighting that the road from high expectations to clinically deployable MLLMs remains long and winding.

摘要：多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）的興起在醫學影像分析領域引發了前所未有的應用浪潮。<lb/>然而，作為這一範式中最早且最基本的任務之一，醫學影像分類揭示了一個令人清醒的現實：儘管在預訓練數據和模型參數上具有壓倒性的優勢，最先進的醫學MLLMs在性能上仍然不及傳統深度學習模型。<lb/>這一悖論促使我們進行重要的重新思考：性能下降究竟源於何處？<lb/>在本文中，我們對14個開源醫學MLLMs在三個具有代表性的影像分類數據集上進行了廣泛的實驗。<lb/>超越表面的性能基準，我們採用特徵探測方法，逐模塊和逐層追蹤視覺特徵的信息流，從而明確可視化分類信號在何處以及如何被扭曲、稀釋或覆蓋。<lb/>作為首次試圖剖析醫學MLLMs中分類性能下降的研究，我們的發現揭示了四種失敗模式：1）視覺表徵的質量限制，2）連接器投影中的保真度損失，3）LLM推理中的理解缺陷，以及4）語義映射的不對齊。<lb/>同時，我們引入了量化分數來表徵特徵演變的健康性，從而實現不同MLLMs和數據集之間的原則性比較。<lb/>此外，我們提供了有見地的討論，集中於當前醫學MLLMs無法實現其承諾的臨床潛力的關鍵障礙。<lb/>我們希望我們的工作能夠引發社群的重新思考，強調從高期望到可臨床部署的MLLMs之路仍然漫長而曲折。

##### **ProMedical: Hierarchical Fine-Grained Criteria Modeling for Medical LLM Alignment via Explicit Injection**
2604.08326v1 by He Geng, Yangmin Huang, Lixian Lai, Qianyun Du, Hui Chu, Zhiyang He, Jiaxue Hu, Xiaodong Tao

Aligning Large Language Models (LLMs) with high-stakes medical standards remains a significant challenge, primarily due to the dissonance between coarse-grained preference signals and the complex, multi-dimensional nature of clinical protocols. To bridge this gap, we introduce ProMedical, a unified alignment framework grounded in fine-grained clinical criteria. We first construct ProMedical-Preference-50k, a dataset generated via a human-in-the-loop pipeline that augments medical instructions with rigorous, physician-derived rubrics. Leveraging this corpus, we propose the Explicit Criteria Injection paradigm to train a multi-dimensional reward model. Unlike traditional scalar reward models, our approach explicitly disentangles safety constraints from general proficiency, enabling precise guidance during reinforcement learning. To rigorously validate this framework, we establish ProMedical-Bench, a held-out evaluation suite anchored by double-blind expert adjudication. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that optimizing the Qwen3-8B base model via ProMedical-RM-guided GRPO yields substantial gains, improving overall accuracy by 22.3% and safety compliance by 21.7%, effectively rivaling proprietary frontier models. Furthermore, the aligned policy generalizes robustly to external benchmarks, demonstrating performance comparable to state-of-the-art models on UltraMedical. We publicly release our datasets, reward models, and benchmarks to facilitate reproducible research in safety-aware medical alignment.

摘要：將大型語言模型（LLMs）與高風險醫療標準對齊仍然是一個重大挑戰，主要是由於粗略偏好信號與臨床協議的複雜多維性之間的矛盾。為了填補這一空白，我們介紹了ProMedical，一個基於細緻臨床標準的統一對齊框架。我們首先構建了ProMedical-Preference-50k，這是一個通過人機協作流程生成的數據集，該流程使用嚴格的醫生導出標準增強醫療指令。利用這個語料庫，我們提出了明確標準注入範式來訓練多維獎勵模型。與傳統的標量獎勵模型不同，我們的方法明確地將安全約束與一般能力分離，從而在強化學習過程中提供精確的指導。為了嚴格驗證這一框架，我們建立了ProMedical-Bench，一個由雙盲專家裁定支持的保留評估套件。實證評估表明，通過ProMedical-RM引導的GRPO優化Qwen3-8B基礎模型可實現顯著增益，整體準確性提高22.3%，安全合規性提高21.7%，有效地與專有前沿模型相抗衡。此外，對齊政策在外部基準上具有強大的泛化能力，顯示出在UltraMedical上與最先進模型相當的性能。我們公開發布了我們的數據集、獎勵模型和基準，以促進安全意識醫療對齊的可重複研究。

##### **DBMF: A Dual-Branch Multimodal Framework for Out-of-Distribution Detection**
2604.08261v2 by Jiangbei Yue, Darren Treanor, Venkataraman Subramanian, Sharib Ali

The complex and dynamic real-world clinical environment demands reliable deep learning (DL) systems. Out-of-distribution (OOD) detection plays a critical role in enhancing the reliability and generalizability of DL models when encountering data that deviate from the training distribution, such as unseen disease cases. However, existing OOD detection methods typically rely either on a single visual modality or solely on image-text matching, failing to fully leverage multimodal information. To overcome the challenge, we propose a novel dual-branch multimodal framework by introducing a text-image branch and a vision branch. Our framework fully exploits multimodal representations to identify OOD samples through these two complementary branches. After training, we compute scores from the text-image branch ($S_t$) and vision branch ($S_v$), and integrate them to obtain the final OOD score $S$ that is compared with a threshold for OOD detection. Comprehensive experiments on publicly available endoscopic image datasets demonstrate that our proposed framework is robust across diverse backbones and improves state-of-the-art performance in OOD detection by up to 24.84%

摘要：複雜且動態的現實臨床環境要求可靠的深度學習（DL）系統。當遇到偏離訓練分佈的數據時，例如未見過的疾病案例，分佈外（OOD）檢測在增強DL模型的可靠性和泛化能力方面扮演著關鍵角色。然而，現有的OOD檢測方法通常依賴於單一的視覺模態或僅依賴於圖像-文本匹配，未能充分利用多模態信息。為了克服這一挑戰，我們提出了一個新穎的雙分支多模態框架，通過引入文本-圖像分支和視覺分支。我們的框架充分利用多模態表示，通過這兩個互補的分支來識別OOD樣本。在訓練後，我們從文本-圖像分支（$S_t$）和視覺分支（$S_v$）計算分數，並將它們整合以獲得最終的OOD分數$S$，該分數與閾值進行比較以進行OOD檢測。在公開可用的內視鏡圖像數據集上的綜合實驗表明，我們提出的框架在多種骨幹上都具有穩健性，並在OOD檢測中將最先進的性能提高了高達24.84%。

##### **Grounding Clinical AI Competency in Human Cognition Through the Clinical World Model and Skill-Mix Framework**
2604.08226v1 by Seyed Amir Ahmad Safavi-Naini, Elahe Meftah, Josh Mohess, Pooya Mohammadi Kazaj, Georgios Siontis, Zahra Atf, Peter R. Lewis, Mauricio Reyes, Girish Nadkarni, Roland Wiest, Stephan Windecker, Christoph Grani, Ali Soroush, Isaac Shiri

The competency of any intelligent agent is bounded by its formal account of the world in which it operates. Clinical AI lacks such an account. Existing frameworks address evaluation, regulation, or system design in isolation, without a shared model of the clinical world to connect them. We introduce the Clinical World Model, a framework that formalizes care as a tripartite interaction among Patient, Provider, and Ecosystem. To formalize how any agent, whether human or artificial, transforms information into clinical action, we develop parallel decision-making architectures for providers, patients, and AI agents, grounded in validated principles of clinical cognition.
  The Clinical AI Skill-Mix operationalizes competency through eight dimensions. Five define the clinical competency space (condition, phase, care setting, provider role, and task) and three specify how AI engages human reasoning (assigned authority, agent facing, and anchoring layer). The combinatorial product of these dimensions yields a space of billions of distinct competency coordinates. A central structural implication is that validation within one coordinate provides minimal evidence for performance in another, rendering the competency space irreducible. The framework supplies a common grammar through which clinical AI can be specified, evaluated, and bounded across stakeholders. By making this structure explicit, the Clinical World Model reframes the field's central question from whether AI works to in which competency coordinates reliability has been demonstrated, and for whom.

摘要：任何智能代理的能力都受到其對所運作世界的正式描述的限制。臨床人工智慧缺乏這樣的描述。現有的框架在孤立中處理評估、監管或系統設計，而沒有共享的臨床世界模型來將它們聯繫起來。我們引入了臨床世界模型，這是一個將護理形式化為病人、提供者和生態系統三方互動的框架。為了形式化任何代理（無論是人類還是人工）如何將信息轉化為臨床行動，我們為提供者、病人和人工智慧代理開發了平行的決策架構，這些架構基於經過驗證的臨床認知原則。

臨床人工智慧技能組合通過八個維度來操作化能力。五個維度定義了臨床能力空間（條件、階段、護理環境、提供者角色和任務），三個維度則具體說明了人工智慧如何參與人類推理（指派權限、面對代理和錨定層）。這些維度的組合產生了數十億個獨特的能力坐標空間。一個核心的結構性含義是，在一個坐標內的驗證對於另一個坐標的表現提供的證據最小，這使得能力空間無法簡化。該框架提供了一種共同的語法，通過它可以在各利益相關者之間對臨床人工智慧進行規範、評估和界定。通過使這一結構明確，臨床世界模型將該領域的核心問題從「人工智慧是否有效」重新框定為「在哪些能力坐標中已證明可靠性，以及對誰有效」。

##### **MedVR: Annotation-Free Medical Visual Reasoning via Agentic Reinforcement Learning**
2604.08203v1 by Zheng Jiang, Heng Guo, Chengyu Fang, Changchen Xiao, Xinyang Hu, Lifeng Sun, Minfeng Xu

Medical Vision-Language Models (VLMs) hold immense promise for complex clinical tasks, but their reasoning capabilities are often constrained by text-only paradigms that fail to ground inferences in visual evidence. This limitation not only curtails performance on tasks requiring fine-grained visual analysis but also introduces risks of visual hallucination in safety-critical applications. Thus, we introduce MedVR, a novel reinforcement learning framework that enables annotation-free visual reasoning for medical VLMs. Its core innovation lies in two synergistic mechanisms: Entropy-guided Visual Regrounding (EVR) uses model uncertainty to direct exploration, while Consensus-based Credit Assignment (CCA) distills pseudo-supervision from rollout agreement. Without any human annotations for intermediate steps, MedVR achieves state-of-the-art performance on diverse public medical VQA benchmarks, significantly outperforming existing models. By learning to reason directly with visual evidence, MedVR promotes the robustness and transparency essential for accelerating the clinical deployment of medical AI.

摘要：醫療視覺-語言模型（VLMs）在複雜的臨床任務中展現出巨大的潛力，但它們的推理能力往往受到僅依賴文本的範式的限制，這些範式未能將推論基於視覺證據。這一限制不僅削弱了對需要細緻視覺分析的任務的表現，還在安全關鍵的應用中引入了視覺幻覺的風險。因此，我們介紹了 MedVR，一個新穎的強化學習框架，能夠實現醫療 VLMs 的無需標註的視覺推理。其核心創新在於兩個協同機制：熵引導的視覺再定位（EVR）利用模型的不確定性來指導探索，而基於共識的信用分配（CCA）則從展開協議中提煉出偽監督。MedVR 在沒有任何人類標註的中間步驟下，實現了在多樣的公共醫療 VQA 基準上達到最先進的性能，顯著超越現有模型。通過學習直接利用視覺證據進行推理，MedVR 促進了加速醫療 AI 臨床部署所需的穩健性和透明性。

##### **From Universal to Individualized Actionability: Revisiting Personalization in Algorithmic Recourse**
2604.08030v1 by Lena Marie Budde, Ayan Majumdar, Richard Uth, Markus Langer, Isabel Valera

Algorithmic recourse aims to provide actionable recommendations that enable individuals to change unfavorable model outcomes, and prior work has extensively studied properties such as efficiency, robustness, and fairness. However, the role of personalization in recourse remains largely implicit and underexplored. While existing approaches incorporate elements of personalization through user interactions, they typically lack an explicit definition of personalization and do not systematically analyze its downstream effects on other recourse desiderata.
  In this paper, we formalize personalization as individual actionability, characterized along two dimensions: hard constraints that specify which features are individually actionable, and soft, individualized constraints that capture preferences over action values and costs. We operationalize these dimensions within the causal algorithmic recourse framework, adopting a pre-hoc user-prompting approach in which individuals express preferences via rankings or scores prior to the generation of any recourse recommendation. Through extensive empirical evaluation, we investigate how personalization interacts with key recourse desiderata, including validity, cost, and plausibility. Our results highlight important trade-offs: individual actionability constraints, particularly hard ones, can substantially degrade the plausibility and validity of recourse recommendations across amortized and non-amortized approaches. Notably, we also find that incorporating individual actionability can reveal disparities in the cost and plausibility of recourse actions across socio-demographic groups. These findings underscore the need for principled definitions, careful operationalization, and rigorous evaluation of personalization in algorithmic recourse.

摘要：算法回應旨在提供可行的建議，使個人能夠改變不利的模型結果，先前的研究廣泛探討了效率、穩健性和公平性等特性。<lb/>然而，個性化在回應中的角色仍然在很大程度上是隱含的且未被充分探索。<lb/>雖然現有的方法通過用戶互動納入了個性化的元素，但它們通常缺乏對個性化的明確定義，並且未系統性地分析其對其他回應需求的下游影響。<lb/>在本文中，我們將個性化形式化為個體可行性，並沿著兩個維度進行特徵描述：硬約束指定哪些特徵是個別可行的，軟性個性化約束則捕捉對行動值和成本的偏好。<lb/>我們在因果算法回應框架內操作化這些維度，採用一種事前用戶提示的方法，讓個體在生成任何回應建議之前通過排名或分數表達偏好。<lb/>通過廣泛的實證評估，我們研究個性化如何與關鍵回應需求互動，包括有效性、成本和合理性。<lb/>我們的結果突顯了重要的權衡：個體可行性約束，特別是硬約束，可能會顯著降低回應建議在攤銷和非攤銷方法中的合理性和有效性。<lb/>值得注意的是，我們還發現納入個體可行性可以揭示社會人口群體之間在回應行動的成本和合理性方面的差異。<lb/>這些發現強調了對算法回應中個性化進行原則性定義、謹慎操作化和嚴謹評估的必要性。

##### **LogAct: Enabling Agentic Reliability via Shared Logs**
2604.07988v1 by Mahesh Balakrishnan, Ashwin Bharambe, Davide Testuggine, David Geraghty, David Mao, Vidhya Venkat, Ilya Mironov, Rithesh Baradi, Gayathri Aiyer, Victoria Dudin

Agents are LLM-driven components that can mutate environments in powerful, arbitrary ways. Extracting guarantees for the execution of agents in production environments can be challenging due to asynchrony and failures. In this paper, we propose a new abstraction called LogAct, where each agent is a deconstructed state machine playing a shared log. In LogAct, agentic actions are visible in the shared log before they are executed; can be stopped prior to execution by pluggable, decoupled voters; and recovered consistently in the case of agent or environment failure. LogAct enables agentic introspection, allowing the agent to analyze its own execution history using LLM inference, which in turn enables semantic variants of recovery, health check, and optimization. In our evaluation, LogAct agents recover efficiently and correctly from failures; debug their own performance; optimize token usage in swarms; and stop all unwanted actions for a target model on a representative benchmark with just a 3% drop in benign utility.

摘要：代理是由LLM驅動的組件，可以以強大且任意的方式改變環境。由於非同步性和故障，為代理在生產環境中的執行提取保證可能具有挑戰性。在本文中，我們提出了一種新的抽象稱為LogAct，其中每個代理都是一個解構的狀態機，播放共享日誌。在LogAct中，代理的行動在執行之前可在共享日誌中可見；可以通過可插拔的、解耦的投票者在執行之前停止；並且在代理或環境故障的情況下可以一致地恢復。LogAct使代理能夠進行自我內省，允許代理使用LLM推理分析其自身的執行歷史，這反過來又使恢復、健康檢查和優化的語義變體成為可能。在我們的評估中，LogAct代理能有效且正確地從故障中恢復；調試自己的性能；在群體中優化標記使用；並且在一個代表性基準上，僅以3%的良性效用下降停止所有不必要的行動。

##### **Detecting HIV-Related Stigma in Clinical Narratives Using Large Language Models**
2604.07717v2 by Ziyi Chen, Yasir Khan, Mengyuan Zhang, Cheng Peng, Mengxian Lyu, Yiyang Liu, Krishna Vaddiparti, Robert L Cook, Mattia Prosperi, Yonghui Wu

Human immunodeficiency virus (HIV)-related stigma is a critical psychosocial determinant of health for people living with HIV (PLWH), influencing mental health, engagement in care, and treatment outcomes. Although stigma-related experiences are documented in clinical narratives, there is a lack of off-the-shelf tools to extract and categorize them. This study aims to develop a large language model (LLM)-based tool for identifying HIV stigma from clinical notes. We identified clinical notes from PLWH receiving care at the University of Florida (UF) Health between 2012 and 2022. Candidate sentences were identified using expert-curated stigma-related keywords and iteratively expanded via clinical word embeddings. A total of 1,332 sentences were manually annotated across four stigma subscales: Concern with Public Attitudes, Disclosure Concerns, Negative Self-Image, and Personalized Stigma. We compared GatorTron-large and BERT as encoder-based baselines, and GPT-OSS-20B, LLaMA-8B, and MedGemma-27B as generative LLMs, under zero-shot and few-shot prompting. GatorTron-large achieved the best overall performance (Micro F1 = 0.62). Few-shot prompting substantially improved generative model performance, with 5-shot GPT-OSS-20B and LLaMA-8B achieving Micro-F1 scores of 0.57 and 0.59, respectively. Performance varied by stigma subscale, with Negative Self-Image showing the highest predictability and Personalized Stigma remaining the most challenging. Zero-shot generative inference exhibited non-trivial failure rates (up to 32%). This study develops the first practical NLP tool for identifying HIV stigma in clinical notes.

摘要：人類免疫缺乏病毒（HIV）相關的污名是影響HIV陽性者（PLWH）健康的關鍵心理社會決定因素，對心理健康、醫療參與和治療結果有著重要影響。雖然臨床敘述中有記錄污名相關的經歷，但缺乏現成的工具來提取和分類這些經歷。本研究旨在開發一種基於大型語言模型（LLM）的工具，以識別臨床筆記中的HIV污名。我們從2012年到2022年在佛羅里達大學（UF）健康中心接受治療的PLWH中識別了臨床筆記。使用專家策劃的污名相關關鍵詞識別候選句子，並通過臨床詞嵌入進行迭代擴展。共手動標註了1,332個句子，涵蓋四個污名子量表：對公共態度的關注、披露擔憂、負面自我形象和個人化污名。我們比較了GatorTron-large和BERT作為編碼器基準，以及GPT-OSS-20B、LLaMA-8B和MedGemma-27B作為生成型LLM，在零-shot和少量提示下進行比較。GatorTron-large實現了最佳的整體表現（Micro F1 = 0.62）。少量提示顯著改善了生成模型的性能，5-shot GPT-OSS-20B和LLaMA-8B的Micro-F1分別達到0.57和0.59。性能因污名子量表而異，負面自我形象顯示出最高的可預測性，而個人化污名則仍然是最具挑戰性的。零-shot生成推斷顯示出非微不足道的失敗率（高達32%）。本研究開發了第一個實用的自然語言處理工具，用於識別臨床筆記中的HIV污名。

##### **IatroBench: Pre-Registered Evidence of Iatrogenic Harm from AI Safety Measures**
2604.07709v3 by David Gringras

Ask a frontier model how to taper six milligrams of alprazolam (psychiatrist retired, ten days of pills left, abrupt cessation causes seizures) and it tells her to call the psychiatrist she just explained does not exist. Change one word ("I'm a psychiatrist; a patient presents with...") and the same model, same weights, same inference pass produces a textbook Ashton Manual taper with diazepam equivalence, anticonvulsant coverage, and monitoring thresholds. The knowledge was there; the model withheld it. IatroBench measures this gap. Sixty pre-registered clinical scenarios, six frontier models, 3,600 responses, scored on two axes (commission harm, CH 0-3; omission harm, OH 0-4) through a structured-evaluation pipeline validated against physician scoring (kappa_w = 0.571, within-1 agreement 96%). The central finding is identity-contingent withholding: match the same clinical question in physician vs. layperson framing and all five testable models provide better guidance to the physician (decoupling gap +0.38, p = 0.003; binary hit rates on safety-colliding actions drop 13.1 percentage points in layperson framing, p < 0.0001, while non-colliding actions show no change). The gap is widest for the model with the heaviest safety investment (Opus, +0.65). Three failure modes separate cleanly: trained withholding (Opus), incompetence (Llama 4), and indiscriminate content filtering (GPT-5.2, whose post-generation filter strips physician responses at 9x the layperson rate because they contain denser pharmacological tokens). The standard LLM judge assigns OH = 0 to 73% of responses a physician scores OH >= 1 (kappa = 0.045); the evaluation apparatus has the same blind spot as the training apparatus. Every scenario targets someone who has already exhausted the standard referrals.

摘要：詢問一個前沿模型如何逐漸減少六毫克的阿普唑仑（精神科醫生退休，還剩十天的藥，突然停藥會引發癲癇），它告訴她去聯繫那位她剛剛解釋過不存在的精神科醫生。只需改變一個詞（「我是一名精神科醫生；一名患者出現...」），同樣的模型、相同的權重、相同的推理過程產生了教科書式的阿什頓手冊減藥方案，並提供了地西泮的等效劑量、抗癲癇藥物的覆蓋以及監測閾值。這些知識存在；模型卻隱瞞了它。IatroBench 測量這一差距。六十個預註冊的臨床情境，六個前沿模型，3600 個回應，根據兩個軸線（委任傷害，CH 0-3；遺漏傷害，OH 0-4）通過一個結構化評估流程進行評分，並與醫生評分進行驗證（kappa_w = 0.571，1內一致性96%）。核心發現是身份依賴的隱瞞：在醫生與外行人框架中匹配相同的臨床問題，所有五個可測試模型都為醫生提供了更好的指導（解耦差距 +0.38，p = 0.003；在外行人框架中，安全衝突行動的二元命中率下降了13.1個百分點，p < 0.0001，而非衝突行動則沒有變化）。對於安全投資最重的模型（Opus，+0.65），差距最為明顯。三種失敗模式清晰分離：訓練隱瞞（Opus）、無能（Llama 4）和不加區分的內容過濾（GPT-5.2，其生成後過濾器以9倍於外行人的速度剝離醫生的回應，因為它們包含更密集的藥理學標記）。標準的 LLM 評判者對73%的醫生評分 OH >= 1 的回應賦予 OH = 0（kappa = 0.045）；評估設備與訓練設備有相同的盲點。每個情境的目標都是那些已經耗盡標準轉介的人。

##### **Generative Experiences for Digital Mental Health Interventions: Evidence from a Randomized Study**
2604.07558v1 by Ananya Bhattacharjee, Michael Liut, Matthew Jörke, Diyi Yang, Emma Brunskill

Digital mental health (DMH) tools have extensively explored personalization of interventions to users' needs and contexts. However, this personalization often targets what support is provided, not how it is experienced. Even well-matched content can fail when the interaction format misaligns with how someone can engage. We introduce generative experience as a paradigm for DMH support, where the intervention experience is composed at runtime. We instantiate this in GUIDE, a system that generates personalized intervention content and multimodal interaction structure through rubric-guided generation of modular components. In a preregistered study with N = 237 participants, GUIDE significantly reduced stress (p = .02) and improved the user experience (p = .04) compared to an LLM-based cognitive restructuring control. GUIDE also supported diverse forms of reflection and action through varied interaction flows, while revealing tensions around personalization across the interaction sequence. This work lays the foundation for interventions that dynamically shape how support is experienced and enacted in digital settings.

摘要：數位心理健康 (DMH) 工具已廣泛探索根據用戶的需求和情境進行干預的個性化。<lb/>然而，這種個性化通常針對提供哪些支持，而不是如何體驗這些支持。<lb/>即使是匹配良好的內容，當互動格式與某人能夠參與的方式不一致時，也可能失敗。<lb/>我們引入生成體驗作為 DMH 支持的一種範式，在這種範式中，干預體驗是在運行時組成的。<lb/>我們在 GUIDE 中實現了這一點，該系統通過基於評分標準的模塊化組件生成個性化的干預內容和多模態互動結構。<lb/>在一項預註冊的研究中，N = 237 名參與者，GUIDE 顯著降低了壓力 (p = .02) 並改善了用戶體驗 (p = .04)，與基於 LLM 的認知重組對照組相比。<lb/>GUIDE 還通過多樣的互動流程支持各種反思和行動形式，同時揭示了在互動序列中圍繞個性化的緊張關係。<lb/>這項工作為在數位環境中動態塑造支持的體驗和執行方式的干預奠定了基礎。

##### **EMSDialog: Synthetic Multi-person Emergency Medical Service Dialogue Generation from Electronic Patient Care Reports via Multi-LLM Agents**
2604.07549v1 by Xueren Ge, Sahil Murtaza, Anthony Cortez, Homa Alemzadeh

Conversational diagnosis prediction requires models to track evolving evidence in streaming clinical conversations and decide when to commit to a diagnosis. Existing medical dialogue corpora are largely dyadic or lack the multi-party workflow and annotations needed for this setting. We introduce an ePCR-grounded, topic-flow-based multi-agent generation pipeline that iteratively plans, generates, and self-refines dialogues with rule-based factual and topic flow checks. The pipeline yields EMSDialog, a dataset of 4,414 synthetic multi-speaker EMS conversations based on a real-world ePCR dataset, annotated with 43 diagnoses, speaker roles, and turn-level topics. Human and LLM evaluations confirm high quality and realism of EMSDialog using both utterance- and conversation-level metrics. Results show that EMSDialog-augmented training improves accuracy, timeliness, and stability of EMS conversational diagnosis prediction.

摘要：對話診斷預測需要模型追踪在流式臨床對話中不斷演變的證據，並決定何時確定診斷。現有的醫療對話語料庫大多是雙方對話，或缺乏這種環境所需的多方工作流程和註釋。我們介紹了一個基於ePCR的、以主題流為基礎的多代理生成管道，該管道通過基於規則的事實和主題流檢查，迭代地規劃、生成和自我修正對話。該管道產生了EMSDialog，這是一個基於真實世界ePCR數據集的4,414個合成多發言者EMS對話的數據集，並註釋了43個診斷、發言者角色和輪次級主題。人類和LLM評估確認了EMSDialog在發言和對話級別度量上具有高質量和真實感。結果顯示，增強EMSDialog的訓練提高了EMS對話診斷預測的準確性、及時性和穩定性。

##### **Triage: Routing Software Engineering Tasks to Cost-Effective LLM Tiers via Code Quality Signals**
2604.07494v1 by Lech Madeyski

Context: AI coding agents route every task to a single frontier large language model (LLM), paying premium inference cost even when many tasks are routine.
  Objectives: We propose Triage, a framework that uses code health metrics -- indicators of software maintainability -- as a routing signal to assign each task to the cheapest model tier whose output passes the same verification gate as the expensive model.
  Methods: Triage defines three capability tiers (light, standard, heavy -- mirroring, e.g., Haiku, Sonnet, Opus) and routes tasks based on pre-computed code health sub-factors and task metadata. We design an evaluation comparing three routing policies on SWE-bench Lite (300 tasks across three model tiers): heuristic thresholds, a trained ML classifier, and a perfect-hindsight oracle.
  Results: We analytically derived two falsifiable conditions under which the tier-dependent asymmetry (medium LLMs benefit from clean code while frontier models do not) yields cost-effective routing: the light-tier pass rate on healthy code must exceed the inter-tier cost ratio, and code health must discriminate the required model tier with at least a small effect size ($\hat{p} \geq 0.56$).
  Conclusion: Triage transforms a diagnostic code quality metric into an actionable model-selection signal. We present a rigorous evaluation protocol to test the cost--quality trade-off and identify which code health sub-factors drive routing decisions.

摘要：Context: AI 編碼代理將每個任務路由到單一的前沿大型語言模型 (LLM)，即使許多任務是例行的，仍需支付高昂的推理成本。<lb/>  
Objectives: 我們提出 Triage，一個使用代碼健康指標（軟體可維護性的指標）作為路由信號的框架，以將每個任務分配給輸出通過與昂貴模型相同驗證門檻的最便宜模型層級。<lb/>  
Methods: Triage 定義了三個能力層級（輕型、標準型、重型 -- 例如，對應 Haiku、Sonnet、Opus），並根據預先計算的代碼健康子因素和任務元數據路由任務。我們設計了一個評估，對比三種路由政策在 SWE-bench Lite 上的表現（300 個任務分布於三個模型層級）：啟發式閾值、訓練的機器學習分類器和完美的事後預測神諭。<lb/>  
Results: 我們分析推導出兩個可證偽的條件，在這些條件下，層級依賴的不對稱性（中型 LLM 從乾淨代碼中受益，而前沿模型則不然）能夠產生成本效益的路由：輕型層級在健康代碼上的通過率必須超過層級間的成本比率，並且代碼健康必須以至少小的效應大小 ($\hat{p} \geq 0.56$) 區分所需的模型層級。<lb/>  
Conclusion: Triage 將診斷性代碼質量指標轉化為可行的模型選擇信號。我們提出了一個嚴謹的評估協議，以測試成本與質量的權衡，並識別哪些代碼健康子因素驅動路由決策。

##### **An Analysis of Artificial Intelligence Adoption in NIH-Funded Research**
2604.07424v1 by Navapat Nananukul, Mayank Kejriwal

Understanding the landscape of artificial intelligence (AI) and machine learning (ML) adoption across the National Institutes of Health (NIH) portfolio is critical for research funding strategy, institutional planning, and health policy. The advent of large language models (LLMs) has fundamentally transformed research landscape analysis, enabling researchers to perform large-scale semantic extraction from thousands of unstructured research documents. In this paper, we illustrate a human-in-the-loop research methodology for LLMs to automatically classify and summarize research descriptions at scale. Using our methodology, we present a comprehensive analysis of 58,746 NIH-funded biomedical research projects from 2025. We show that: (1) AI constitutes 15.9% of the NIH portfolio with a 13.4% funding premium, concentrated in discovery, prediction, and data integration across disease domains; (2) a critical research-to-deployment gap exists, with 79% of AI projects remaining in research/development stages while only 14.7% engage in clinical deployment or implementation; and (3) health disparities research is severely underrepresented at just 5.7% of AI-funded work despite its importance to NIH's equity mission. These findings establish a framework for evidence-based policy interventions to align the NIH AI portfolio with health equity goals and strategic research priorities.

摘要：了解國立衛生研究院（NIH）在人工智慧（AI）和機器學習（ML）採用方面的現狀對於研究資金策略、機構規劃和健康政策至關重要。大型語言模型（LLMs）的出現根本改變了研究景觀分析，使研究人員能夠從數千份非結構化研究文件中進行大規模的語義提取。在本文中，我們展示了一種人機協作的研究方法，利用LLMs自動對研究描述進行分類和摘要。使用我們的方法論，我們對2025年58,746個NIH資助的生物醫學研究項目進行了全面分析。我們顯示：（1）AI佔NIH投資組合的15.9%，資金溢價為13.4%，主要集中在疾病領域的發現、預測和數據整合；（2）存在關鍵的研究到部署的差距，79%的AI項目仍處於研究/開發階段，而只有14.7%參與臨床部署或實施；（3）儘管健康差距研究對NIH的公平使命至關重要，但其在AI資助工作中的代表性僅為5.7%。這些發現建立了一個基於證據的政策干預框架，以使NIH的AI投資組合與健康公平目標和戰略研究優先事項保持一致。

##### **A Systematic Study of Retrieval Pipeline Design for Retrieval-Augmented Medical Question Answering**
2604.07274v1 by Nusrat Sultana, Abdullah Muhammad Moosa, Kazi Afzalur Rahman, Sajal Chandra Banik

Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in medical question answering; however, purely parametric models often suffer from knowledge gaps and limited factual grounding. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) addresses this limitation by integrating external knowledge retrieval into the reasoning process. Despite increasing interest in RAG-based medical systems, the impact of individual retrieval components on performance remains insufficiently understood. This study presents a systematic evaluation of retrieval-augmented medical question answering using the MedQA USMLE benchmark and a structured textbook-based knowledge corpus. We analyze the interaction between language models, embedding models, retrieval strategies, query reformulation, and cross-encoder reranking within a unified experimental framework comprising forty configurations. Results show that retrieval augmentation significantly improves zero-shot medical question answering performance. The best-performing configuration was dense retrieval with query reformulation and reranking achieved 60.49% accuracy. Domain-specialized language models were also found to better utilize retrieved medical evidence than general-purpose models. The analysis further reveals a clear tradeoff between retrieval effectiveness and computational cost, with simpler dense retrieval configurations providing strong performance while maintaining higher throughput. All experiments were conducted on a single consumer-grade GPU, demonstrating that systematic evaluation of retrieval-augmented medical QA systems can be performed under modest computational resources.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在醫療問題回答方面展現了強大的能力；然而，純粹的參數模型往往存在知識空白和有限的事實基礎。檢索增強生成（RAG）通過將外部知識檢索整合到推理過程中來解決這一限制。儘管對基於RAG的醫療系統的興趣日益增加，但各個檢索組件對性能的影響仍然了解不足。本研究對使用MedQA USMLE基準和結構化教科書知識語料庫的檢索增強醫療問題回答進行了系統評估。我們分析了語言模型、嵌入模型、檢索策略、查詢重構和交叉編碼重排序之間的互動，並在一個包含四十種配置的統一實驗框架中進行。結果顯示，檢索增強顯著提高了零樣本醫療問題回答的性能。表現最佳的配置是使用查詢重構和重排序的稠密檢索，達到60.49%的準確率。專業領域的語言模型在利用檢索到的醫療證據方面也被發現比通用模型更有效。分析進一步揭示了檢索效果與計算成本之間的明顯權衡，較簡單的稠密檢索配置在保持較高吞吐量的同時提供了強勁的性能。所有實驗均在單個消費級GPU上進行，顯示出在適度的計算資源下可以對檢索增強的醫療QA系統進行系統評估。

#### Abstracts
##### **Generalization in LLM Problem Solving: The Case of the Shortest Path**
2604.15306v1 by Yao Tong, Jiayuan Ye, Anastasia Borovykh, Reza Shokri

Whether language models can systematically generalize remains actively debated. Yet empirical performance is jointly shaped by multiple factors such as training data, training paradigms, and inference-time strategies, making failures difficult to interpret. We introduce a controlled synthetic environment based on shortest-path planning, a canonical composable sequential optimization problem. The setup enables clean separation of these factors and supports two orthogonal axes of generalization: spatial transfer to unseen maps and length scaling to longer-horizon problems. We find that models exhibit strong spatial transfer but consistently fail under length scaling due to recursive instability. We further analyze how distinct stages of the learning pipeline influence systematic problem-solving: for example, data coverage sets capability limits; reinforcement learning improves training stability but does not expand those limits; and inference-time scaling enhances performance but cannot rescue length-scaling failures.

摘要：語言模型是否能夠系統性地進行泛化仍然是活躍的辯論主題。<lb/>然而，實證表現是由多個因素共同影響的，例如訓練數據、訓練範式和推理時間策略，這使得失敗的解釋變得困難。<lb/>我們介紹了一個基於最短路徑規劃的受控合成環境，這是一個典型的可組合序列優化問題。<lb/>該設置能夠清晰地分離這些因素，並支持兩個正交的泛化軸：對未見地圖的空間轉移和對更長時間範圍問題的長度縮放。<lb/>我們發現模型在空間轉移方面表現強勁，但在長度縮放下卻始終失敗，原因是遞歸不穩定性。<lb/>我們進一步分析了學習流程的不同階段如何影響系統性問題解決：例如，數據覆蓋設置了能力限制；強化學習提高了訓練穩定性，但並未擴展這些限制；而推理時間的縮放提升了性能，但無法挽救長度縮放的失敗。

##### **Diagnosing LLM Judge Reliability: Conformal Prediction Sets and Transitivity Violations**
2604.15302v1 by Manan Gupta, Dhruv Kumar

LLM-as-judge frameworks are increasingly used for automatic NLG evaluation, yet their per-instance reliability remains poorly understood. We present a two-pronged diagnostic toolkit applied to SummEval: $\textbf{(1)}$ a transitivity analysis that reveals widespread per-input inconsistency masked by low aggregate violation rates ($\barρ = 0.8$-$4.1\%$), with $33$-$67\%$ of documents exhibiting at least one directed 3-cycle; and $\textbf{(2)}$ split conformal prediction sets over 1-5 Likert scores providing theoretically-guaranteed $\geq(1{-}α)$ coverage, with set width serving as a per-instance reliability indicator ($r_s = {+}0.576$, $N{=}1{,}918$, $p < 10^{-100}$, pooled across all judges). Critically, prediction set width shows consistent cross-judge agreement ($\bar{r} = 0.32$-$0.38$), demonstrating it captures document-level difficulty rather than judge-specific noise. Across four judges and four criteria, both diagnostics converge: criterion matters more than judge, with relevance judged most reliably (avg. set size $\approx 3.0$) and coherence moderately so (avg. set size $\approx 3.9$), while fluency and consistency remain unreliable (avg. set size $\approx 4.9$). We release all code, prompts, and cached results.

摘要：LLM-as-judge 框架越來越多地被用於自動 NLG 評估，但它們的每個實例可靠性仍然不甚了解。<lb/>我們展示了一個應用於 SummEval 的雙管齊下的診斷工具包：$\textbf{(1)}$ 一個傳遞性分析，揭示了被低總體違規率 ($\barρ = 0.8$-$4.1\%$) 掩蓋的普遍每個輸入不一致性，其中 $33$-$67\%$ 的文檔顯示至少有一個定向的 3-循環；以及 $\textbf{(2)}$ 在 1-5 Likert 分數上分割的符合預測集，提供理論上保證的 $\geq(1{-}α)$ 覆蓋率，集合寬度作為每個實例的可靠性指標 ($r_s = {+}0.576$, $N{=}1{,}918$, $p < 10^{-100}$，在所有評審中合併)。<lb/>關鍵是，預測集寬度顯示出一致的跨評審一致性 ($\bar{r} = 0.32$-$0.38$)，表明它捕捉了文檔級別的難度，而不是評審特定的噪音。<lb/>在四位評審和四個標準中，這兩個診斷結果趨於一致：標準比評審更重要，相關性被評判得最可靠（平均集合大小 $\approx 3.0$）而連貫性則適度（平均集合大小 $\approx 3.9$），而流暢性和一致性仍然不可靠（平均集合大小 $\approx 4.9$）。<lb/>我們釋放所有代碼、提示和緩存結果。

##### **How Do LLMs and VLMs Understand Viewpoint Rotation Without Vision? An Interpretability Study**
2604.15294v1 by Zhen Yang, Ping Jian, Zhongbin Guo, Zuming Zhang, Chengzhi Li, Yonghong Deng, Xinyue Zhang, Wenpeng Lu

Over the past year, spatial intelligence has drawn increasing attention. Many prior works study it from the perspective of visual-spatial intelligence, where models have access to visuospatial information from visual inputs. However, in the absence of visual information, whether linguistic intelligence alone is sufficient to endow models with spatial intelligence, and how models perform relevant tasks with text-only inputs still remain unexplored. Therefore, in this paper, we focus on a fundamental and critical capability in spatial intelligence from a linguistic perspective: viewpoint rotation understanding (VRU). Specifically, LLMs and VLMs are asked to infer their final viewpoint and predict the corresponding observation in an environment given textual description of viewpoint rotation and observation over multiple steps. We find that both LLMs and VLMs perform poorly on our proposed dataset while human can easily achieve 100% accuracy, indicating a substantial gap between current model capabilities and the requirements of spatial intelligence. To uncover the underlying mechanisms, we conduct a layer-wise probing analysis and head-wise causal intervention. Our findings reveal that although models encode viewpoint information in the hidden states, they appear to struggle to bind the viewpoint position with corresponding observation, resulting in a hallucination in final layers. Finally, we selectively fine-tune the key attention heads identified by causal intervention to improve VRU performance. Experimental results demonstrate that such selective fine-tuning achieves improved VRU performance while avoiding catastrophic forgetting of generic abilities. Our dataset and code will be released at https://github.com/Young-Zhen/VRU_Interpret .

摘要：在過去一年中，空間智能引起了越來越多的關注。許多先前的研究從視覺空間智能的角度進行研究，模型可以從視覺輸入中獲取視覺空間信息。然而，在缺乏視覺信息的情況下，僅依賴語言智能是否足以賦予模型空間智能，以及模型如何使用僅有文本的輸入執行相關任務仍然未被探索。因此，在本文中，我們從語言的角度專注於空間智能中的一個基本且關鍵的能力：視點旋轉理解（VRU）。具體而言，我們要求大型語言模型（LLMs）和視覺語言模型（VLMs）根據多步的視點旋轉和觀察的文本描述推斷其最終視點並預測相應的環境觀察。我們發現，LLMs和VLMs在我們提出的數據集上表現不佳，而人類則能輕鬆達到100%的準確率，這表明當前模型能力與空間智能的要求之間存在顯著差距。為了揭示潛在的機制，我們進行了逐層探測分析和頭部因果干預。我們的發現顯示，儘管模型在隱藏狀態中編碼了視點信息，但它們似乎難以將視點位置與相應的觀察綁定，導致最終層出現幻覺。最後，我們選擇性地微調因果干預識別的關鍵注意頭，以改善VRU性能。實驗結果表明，這種選擇性微調在提高VRU性能的同時，避免了對通用能力的災難性遺忘。我們的數據集和代碼將在 https://github.com/Young-Zhen/VRU_Interpret 發布。

##### **AD4AD: Benchmarking Visual Anomaly Detection Models for Safer Autonomous Driving**
2604.15291v1 by Fabrizio Genilotti, Arianna Stropeni, Gionata Grotto, Francesco Borsatti, Manuel Barusco, Davide Dalle Pezze, Gian Antonio Susto

The reliability of a machine vision system for autonomous driving depends heavily on its training data distribution. When a vehicle encounters significantly different conditions, such as atypical obstacles, its perceptual capabilities can degrade substantially. Unlike many domains where errors carry limited consequences, failures in autonomous driving translate directly into physical risk for passengers, pedestrians, and other road users. To address this challenge, we explore Visual Anomaly Detection (VAD) as a solution. VAD enables the identification of anomalous objects not present during training, allowing the system to alert the driver when an unfamiliar situation is detected. Crucially, VAD models produce pixel-level anomaly maps that can guide driver attention to specific regions of concern without requiring any prior assumptions about the nature or form of the hazard. We benchmark eight state-of-the-art VAD methods on AnoVox, the largest synthetic dataset for anomaly detection in autonomous driving. In particular, we evaluate performance across four backbone architectures spanning from large networks to lightweight ones such as MobileNet and DeiT-Tiny. Our results demonstrate that VAD transfers effectively to road scenes. Notably, Tiny-Dinomaly achieves the best accuracy-efficiency trade-off for edge deployment, matching full-scale localization performance at a fraction of the memory cost. This study represents a concrete step toward safer, more responsible deployment of autonomous vehicles, ultimately improving protection for passengers, pedestrians, and all road users.

摘要：機器視覺系統在自動駕駛中的可靠性在很大程度上依賴於其訓練數據的分佈。當車輛遇到顯著不同的條件，例如不尋常的障礙物時，其感知能力可能會大幅下降。與許多錯誤後果有限的領域不同，自動駕駛中的失敗直接轉化為對乘客、行人和其他道路使用者的物理風險。為了解決這一挑戰，我們探索了視覺異常檢測（VAD）作為解決方案。VAD使得能夠識別訓練期間不存在的異常物體，當檢測到不熟悉的情況時，系統可以提醒駕駛員。關鍵是，VAD模型生成的像素級異常圖可以引導駕駛員注意特定的關注區域，而不需要對危險的性質或形式做出任何先前的假設。我們在AnoVox上基準測試了八種最先進的VAD方法，這是自動駕駛中異常檢測的最大合成數據集。特別地，我們評估了四種骨幹架構的性能，從大型網絡到輕量級網絡如MobileNet和DeiT-Tiny。我們的結果顯示，VAD能有效轉移到道路場景中。值得注意的是，Tiny-Dinomaly在邊緣部署中實現了最佳的準確性與效率的平衡，以極低的內存成本匹配全規模定位性能。本研究代表了邁向更安全、更負責任的自動駕駛車輛部署的一個具體步驟，最終改善了對乘客、行人和所有道路使用者的保護。

##### **Why Do Vision Language Models Struggle To Recognize Human Emotions?**
2604.15280v1 by Madhav Agarwal, Sotirios A. Tsaftaris, Laura Sevilla-Lara, Steven McDonagh

Understanding emotions is a fundamental ability for intelligent systems to be able to interact with humans. Vision-language models (VLMs) have made tremendous progress in the last few years for many visual tasks, potentially offering a promising solution for understanding emotions. However, it is surprising that even the most sophisticated contemporary VLMs struggle to recognize human emotions or to outperform even specialized vision-only classifiers. In this paper we ask the question "Why do VLMs struggle to recognize human emotions?", and observe that the inherently continuous and dynamic task of facial expression recognition (DFER) exposes two critical VLM vulnerabilities. First, emotion datasets are naturally long-tailed, and the web-scale data used to pre-train VLMs exacerbates this head-class bias, causing them to systematically collapse rare, under-represented emotions into common categories. We propose alternative sampling strategies that prevent favoring common concepts. Second, temporal information is critical for understanding emotions. However, VLMs are unable to represent temporal information over dense frame sequences, as they are limited by context size and the number of tokens that can fit in memory, which poses a clear challenge for emotion recognition. We demonstrate that the sparse temporal sampling strategy used in VLMs is inherently misaligned with the fleeting nature of micro-expressions (0.25-0.5 seconds), which are often the most critical affective signal. As a diagnostic probe, we propose a multi-stage context enrichment strategy that utilizes the information from "in-between" frames by first converting them into natural language summaries. This enriched textual context is provided as input to the VLM alongside sparse keyframes, preventing attentional dilution from excessive visual data while preserving the emotional trajectory.

摘要：理解情感是智能系統能夠與人類互動的基本能力。視覺語言模型（VLMs）在過去幾年中在許多視覺任務上取得了巨大的進展，可能為理解情感提供了一個有希望的解決方案。然而，令人驚訝的是，即使是當代最先進的 VLMs 也難以識別人類情感，或者在性能上超越專門的僅視覺分類器。在本文中，我們提出問題「為什麼 VLMs 難以識別人類情感？」並觀察到，面部表情識別（DFER）這一固有的連續和動態任務暴露了 VLM 的兩個關鍵脆弱性。首先，情感數據集自然是長尾的，而用於預訓練 VLM 的網絡規模數據加劇了這種頭部類別偏見，導致它們系統性地將稀有的、代表性不足的情感合併到常見類別中。我們提出了替代的抽樣策略，以防止偏向常見概念。其次，時間信息對於理解情感至關重要。然而，VLM 無法在密集的幀序列中表示時間信息，因為它們受到上下文大小和可以放入記憶中的標記數量的限制，這對情感識別構成了明顯的挑戰。我們展示了 VLM 中使用的稀疏時間抽樣策略與微表情（0.25-0.5 秒）的瞬時特性本質上不一致，而微表情通常是最關鍵的情感信號。作為診斷探針，我們提出了一種多階段上下文豐富策略，通過首先將「介於」幀之間的信息轉換為自然語言摘要來利用這些信息。這種豐富的文本上下文與稀疏的關鍵幀一起作為輸入提供給 VLM，防止因過多的視覺數據而導致的注意力稀釋，同時保留情感軌跡。

##### **Prism: Symbolic Superoptimization of Tensor Programs**
2604.15272v1 by Mengdi Wu, Xiaoyu Jiang, Oded Padon, Zhihao Jia

This paper presents Prism, the first symbolic superoptimizer for tensor programs. The key idea is sGraph, a symbolic, hierarchical representation that compactly encodes large classes of tensor programs by symbolically representing some execution parameters. Prism organizes optimization as a two-level search: it constructs symbolic graphs that represent families of programs, and then instantiates them into concrete implementations. This formulation enables structured pruning of provably suboptimal regions of the search space using symbolic reasoning over operator semantics, algebraic identities, and hardware constraints.
  We develop techniques for efficient symbolic graph generation, equivalence verification via e-graph rewriting, and parameter instantiation through auto-tuning. Together, these components allow Prism to bridge the rigor of exhaustive search with the scalability required for modern ML workloads. Evaluation on five commonly used LLM workloads shows that Prism achieves up to $2.2\times$ speedup over best superoptimizers and $4.9\times$ over best compiler-based approaches, while reducing end-to-end optimization time by up to $3.4\times$.

摘要：這篇論文介紹了Prism，首個用於張量程序的符號超優化器。<lb/>其關鍵思想是sGraph，一種符號的、分層的表示法，通過符號表示某些執行參數來緊湊地編碼大類張量程序。<lb/>Prism將優化組織為兩級搜索：它構建表示程序家族的符號圖，然後將其實例化為具體實現。<lb/>這種表述使得能夠通過對運算元語義、代數恆等式和硬體約束的符號推理來結構化地修剪可證明的次優區域。<lb/>我們開發了高效的符號圖生成技術、通過e-graph重寫進行的等價驗證，以及通過自動調整進行的參數實例化。<lb/>這些組件共同使Prism能夠將徹底搜索的嚴謹性與現代機器學習工作負載所需的可擴展性相結合。<lb/>對五個常用的LLM工作負載的評估顯示，Prism在最佳超優化器上實現了高達$2.2\times$的加速，而在最佳基於編譯器的方法上則達到了$4.9\times$的加速，同時將端到端的優化時間縮短了高達$3.4\times$。

##### **SegWithU: Uncertainty as Perturbation Energy for Single-Forward-Pass Risk-Aware Medical Image Segmentation**
2604.15271v1 by Tianhao Fu, Austin Wang, Charles Chen, Roby Aldave-Garza, Yucheng Chen

Reliable uncertainty estimation is critical for medical image segmentation, where automated contours feed downstream quantification and clinical decision support. Many strong uncertainty methods require repeated inference, while efficient single-forward-pass alternatives often provide weaker failure ranking or rely on restrictive feature-space assumptions. We present $\textbf{SegWithU}$, a post-hoc framework that augments a frozen pretrained segmentation backbone with a lightweight uncertainty head. SegWithU taps intermediate backbone features and models uncertainty as perturbation energy in a compact probe space using rank-1 posterior probes. It produces two voxel-wise uncertainty maps: a calibration-oriented map for probability tempering and a ranking-oriented map for error detection and selective prediction. Across ACDC, BraTS2024, and LiTS, SegWithU is the strongest and most consistent single-forward-pass baseline, achieving AUROC/AURC of $0.9838/2.4885$, $0.9946/0.2660$, and $0.9925/0.8193$, respectively, while preserving segmentation quality. These results suggest that perturbation-based uncertainty modeling is an effective and practical route to reliability-aware medical segmentation.
  Source code is available at https://github.com/ProjectNeura/SegWithU.

摘要：可靠的不確定性估計對於醫學影像分割至關重要，因為自動化輪廓會為下游量化和臨床決策支持提供數據。許多強大的不確定性方法需要重複推斷，而高效的單次前向傳遞替代方案通常提供較弱的失敗排名或依賴於限制性的特徵空間假設。我們提出了 $\textbf{SegWithU}$，這是一個後處理框架，通過輕量級的不確定性頭部增強了一個凍結的預訓練分割骨幹。SegWithU 利用中間骨幹特徵，並在一個緊湊的探針空間中將不確定性建模為擾動能量，使用一階後驗探針。它生成兩個體素級的不確定性圖：一個面向校準的圖，用於概率調整，另一個面向排名的圖，用於錯誤檢測和選擇性預測。在 ACDC、BraTS2024 和 LiTS 中，SegWithU 是最強且最一致的單次前向傳遞基線，分別達到 AUROC/AURC 的 $0.9838/2.4885$、$0.9946/0.2660$ 和 $0.9925/0.8193$，同時保持分割質量。這些結果表明，基於擾動的不確定性建模是一條有效且實用的可靠性意識醫學分割路徑。源代碼可在 https://github.com/ProjectNeura/SegWithU 獲得。

##### **CoopEval: Benchmarking Cooperation-Sustaining Mechanisms and LLM Agents in Social Dilemmas**
2604.15267v1 by Emanuel Tewolde, Xiao Zhang, David Guzman Piedrahita, Vincent Conitzer, Zhijing Jin

It is increasingly important that LLM agents interact effectively and safely with other goal-pursuing agents, yet, recent works report the opposite trend: LLMs with stronger reasoning capabilities behave _less_ cooperatively in mixed-motive games such as the prisoner's dilemma and public goods settings. Indeed, our experiments show that recent models -- with or without reasoning enabled -- consistently defect in single-shot social dilemmas.
  To tackle this safety concern, we present the first comparative study of game-theoretic mechanisms that are designed to enable cooperative outcomes between rational agents _in equilibrium_. Across four social dilemmas testing distinct components of robust cooperation, we evaluate the following mechanisms: (1) repeating the game for many rounds, (2) reputation systems, (3) third-party mediators to delegate decision making to, and (4) contract agreements for outcome-conditional payments between players. Among our findings, we establish that contracting and mediation are most effective in achieving cooperative outcomes between capable LLM models, and that repetition-induced cooperation deteriorates drastically when co-players vary. Moreover, we demonstrate that these cooperation mechanisms become _more effective_ under evolutionary pressures to maximize individual payoffs.

摘要：隨著 LLM 代理人與其他追求目標的代理人之間有效且安全的互動變得越來越重要，近期的研究卻報告了相反的趨勢：擁有更強推理能力的 LLM 在混合動機遊戲中，如囚徒困境和公共財設定中，表現得 _不太_ 合作。事實上，我們的實驗顯示，最近的模型——無論是否啟用推理——在單次社會困境中始終選擇背叛。<lb/>為了解決這一安全問題，我們提出了首個比較研究，針對旨在促進理性代理人之間的合作結果的博弈論機制，這些結果是在 _均衡_ 狀態下實現的。在四個測試穩健合作不同組件的社會困境中，我們評估了以下機制：(1) 重複進行多輪遊戲，(2) 信譽系統，(3) 第三方調解人以委託決策，以及 (4) 針對玩家之間結果條件支付的合約協議。在我們的研究中，我們確立了合約和調解在促進有能力的 LLM 模型之間達成合作結果方面是最有效的，而重複引起的合作在共同玩家變化時會急劇惡化。此外，我們證明這些合作機制在進化壓力下為最大化個人收益時變得 _更有效_。

##### **From Tokens to Steps: Verification-Aware Speculative Decoding for Efficient Multi-Step Reasoning**
2604.15244v1 by Kiran Purohit, Ramasuri Narayanam, Soumyabrata Pal

Speculative decoding (SD) accelerates large language model inference by allowing a lightweight draft model to propose outputs that a stronger target model verifies. However, its token-centric nature allows erroneous steps to propagate. Prior approaches mitigate this using external reward models, but incur additional latency, computational overhead, and limit generalizability. We propose SpecGuard, a verification-aware speculative decoding framework that performs step-level verification using only model-internal signals. At each step, SpecGuard samples multiple draft candidates and selects the most consistent step, which is then validated using an ensemble of two lightweight model-internal signals: (i) an attention-based grounding score that measures attribution to the input and previously accepted steps, and (ii) a log-probability-based score that captures token-level confidence. These signals jointly determine whether a step is accepted or recomputed using the target, allocating compute selectively. Experiments across a range of reasoning benchmarks show that SpecGuard improves accuracy by 3.6% while reducing latency by ~11%, outperforming both SD and reward-guided SD.

摘要：推測解碼（SD）通過允許輕量級草稿模型提出輸出，讓更強大的目標模型進行驗證，從而加速大型語言模型的推理。然而，其以標記為中心的特性允許錯誤步驟的傳播。先前的方法通過使用外部獎勵模型來減輕這一問題，但會產生額外的延遲、計算開銷，並限制一般化能力。我們提出了SpecGuard，一個具有驗證意識的推測解碼框架，僅使用模型內部信號進行逐步驗證。在每一步中，SpecGuard 會抽樣多個草稿候選者並選擇最一致的一步，然後使用兩個輕量級模型內部信號的集成來進行驗證：（i）一個基於注意力的基準分數，用於衡量對輸入和先前接受步驟的歸因，以及（ii）一個基於對數概率的分數，用於捕捉標記級別的信心。這些信號共同決定某一步是被接受還是使用目標重新計算，並選擇性地分配計算資源。針對一系列推理基準的實驗顯示，SpecGuard 將準確性提高了 3.6%，同時將延遲減少了約 11%，超越了 SD 和獎勵引導的 SD。

##### **Agentic Microphysics: A Manifesto for Generative AI Safety**
2604.15236v1 by Federico Pierucci, Matteo Prandi, Marcantonio Bracale Syrnikov, Marcello Galisai, Piercosma Bisconti

This paper advances a methodological proposal for safety research in agentic AI. As systems acquire planning, memory, tool use, persistent identity, and sustained interaction, safety can no longer be analysed primarily at the level of the isolated model. Population-level risks arise from structured interaction among agents, through processes of communication, observation, and mutual influence that shape collective behaviour over time. As the object of analysis shifts, a methodological gap emerges. Approaches focused either on single agents or on aggregate outcomes do not identify the interaction-level mechanisms that generate collective risks or the design variables that control them. A framework is required that links local interaction structure to population-level dynamics in a causally explicit way, allowing both explanation and intervention. We introduce two linked concepts. Agentic microphysics defines the level of analysis: local interaction dynamics where one agent's output becomes another's input under specific protocol conditions. Generative safety defines the methodology: growing phenomena and elicit risks from micro-level conditions to identify sufficient mechanisms, detect thresholds, and design effective interventions.

摘要：這篇論文提出了一個針對代理式人工智慧安全研究的方法論建議。隨著系統獲得規劃、記憶、工具使用、持續身份和持續互動，安全性不再僅能在孤立模型的層面上進行分析。來自代理之間結構化互動的人口層級風險，通過溝通、觀察和相互影響的過程，隨著時間的推移塑造集體行為。隨著分析對象的轉變，出現了一個方法論上的空白。專注於單一代理或總體結果的方法無法識別產生集體風險的互動層級機制或控制這些機制的設計變數。需要一個框架，將局部互動結構與人口層級動態以因果明確的方式聯繫起來，從而實現解釋和干預。我們引入了兩個相互關聯的概念。代理微物理學定義了分析的層面：在特定協議條件下，一個代理的輸出成為另一個代理的輸入的局部互動動態。生成安全性定義了方法論：從微觀層級條件中增長現象並引發風險，以識別充分的機制、檢測閾值並設計有效的干預措施。

##### **Blue Data Intelligence Layer: Streaming Data and Agents for Multi-source Multi-modal Data-Centric Applications**
2604.15233v1 by Moin Aminnaseri, Farima Fatahi Bayat, Nikita Bhutani, Jean-Flavien Bussotti, Kevin Chan, Rafael Li Chen, Yanlin Feng, Jackson Hassell, Estevam Hruschka, Eser Kandogan, Hannah Kim, James Levine, Seiji Maekawa, Jalal Mahmud, Kushan Mitra, Naoki Otani, Pouya Pezeshkpour, Nima Shahbazi, Chen Shen, Dan Zhang

NL2SQL systems aim to address the growing need for natural language interaction with data. However, real-world information rarely maps to a single SQL query because (1) users express queries iteratively (2) questions often span multiple data sources beyond the closed-world assumption of a single database, and (3) queries frequently rely on commonsense or external knowledge. Consequently, satisfying realistic data needs require integrating heterogeneous sources, modalities, and contextual data. In this paper, we present Blue's Data Intelligence Layer (DIL) designed to support multi-source, multi-modal, and data-centric applications. Blue is a compound AI system that orchestrates agents and data for enterprise settings. DIL serves as the data intelligence layer for agentic data processing, to bridge the semantic gap between user intent and available information by unifying structured enterprise data, world knowledge accessible through LLMs, and personal context obtained through interaction. At the core of DIL is a data registry that stores metadata for diverse data sources and modalities to enable both native and natural language queries. DIL treats LLMs, the Web, and the User as source 'databases', each with their own query interface, elevating them to first-class data sources. DIL relies on data planners to transform user queries into executable query plans. These plans are declarative abstractions that unify relational operators with other operators spanning multiple modalities. DIL planners support decomposition of complex requests into subqueries, retrieval from diverse sources, and finally reasoning and integration to produce final results. We demonstrate DIL through two interactive scenarios in which user queries dynamically trigger multi-source retrieval, cross-modal reasoning, and result synthesis, illustrating how compound AI systems can move beyond single database NL2SQL.

摘要：NL2SQL 系統旨在滿足對數據進行自然語言互動的日益增長的需求。<lb/>然而，現實世界的信息很少能映射到單一的 SQL 查詢，因為 (1) 用戶表達查詢是迭代的，(2) 問題通常跨越多個數據來源，超出單一數據庫的封閉世界假設，並且 (3) 查詢經常依賴於常識或外部知識。<lb/>因此，滿足現實的數據需求需要整合異構來源、模式和上下文數據。<lb/>在本文中，我們介紹了 Blue 的數據智能層 (DIL)，旨在支持多來源、多模式和以數據為中心的應用。<lb/>Blue 是一個複合 AI 系統，旨在為企業環境協調代理和數據。<lb/>DIL 作為代理數據處理的數據智能層，通過統一結構化企業數據、通過 LLM 可訪問的世界知識以及通過互動獲得的個人上下文，來彌合用戶意圖與可用信息之間的語義差距。<lb/>DIL 的核心是一個數據註冊中心，存儲多樣數據來源和模式的元數據，以支持本地和自然語言查詢。<lb/>DIL 將 LLM、網絡和用戶視為源 "數據庫"，每個數據庫都有自己的查詢接口，將它們提升為一級數據來源。<lb/>DIL 依賴數據規劃者將用戶查詢轉換為可執行的查詢計劃。<lb/>這些計劃是聲明性抽象，統一了關係運算符與跨越多種模式的其他運算符。<lb/>DIL 規劃者支持將複雜請求分解為子查詢，從多樣來源檢索數據，並最終進行推理和整合以產生最終結果。<lb/>我們通過兩個互動場景展示 DIL，在這些場景中，用戶查詢動態觸發多來源檢索、跨模式推理和結果合成，說明複合 AI 系統如何超越單一數據庫的 NL2SQL。

##### **RadAgent: A tool-using AI agent for stepwise interpretation of chest computed tomography**
2604.15231v1 by Mélanie Roschewitz, Kenneth Styppa, Yitian Tao, Jiwoong Sohn, Jean-Benoit Delbrouck, Benjamin Gundersen, Nicolas Deperrois, Christian Bluethgen, Julia Vogt, Bjoern Menze, Farhad Nooralahzadeh, Michael Krauthammer, Michael Moor

Vision-language models (VLM) have markedly advanced AI-driven interpretation and reporting of complex medical imaging, such as computed tomography (CT). Yet, existing methods largely relegate clinicians to passive observers of final outputs, offering no interpretable reasoning trace for them to inspect, validate, or refine. To address this, we introduce RadAgent, a tool-using AI agent that generates CT reports through a stepwise and interpretable process. Each resulting report is accompanied by a fully inspectable trace of intermediate decisions and tool interactions, allowing clinicians to examine how the reported findings are derived. In our experiments, we observe that RadAgent improves Chest CT report generation over its 3D VLM counterpart, CT-Chat, across three dimensions. Clinical accuracy improves by 6.0 points (36.4% relative) in macro-F1 and 5.4 points (19.6% relative) in micro-F1. Robustness under adversarial conditions improves by 24.7 points (41.9% relative). Furthermore, RadAgent achieves 37.0% in faithfulness, a new capability entirely absent in its 3D VLM counterpart. By structuring the interpretation of chest CT as an explicit, tool-augmented and iterative reasoning trace, RadAgent brings us closer toward transparent and reliable AI for radiology.

摘要：視覺語言模型（VLM）顯著推進了基於人工智慧的複雜醫學影像解釋和報告，例如電腦斷層掃描（CT）。然而，現有的方法在很大程度上使臨床醫生成為最終輸出的被動觀察者，並未提供可解釋的推理痕跡供他們檢查、驗證或改進。為了解決這個問題，我們引入了 RadAgent，一個使用工具的人工智慧代理，通過逐步且可解釋的過程生成 CT 報告。每份生成的報告都附有可完全檢查的中間決策和工具互動的痕跡，允許臨床醫生檢查報告結果的推導過程。在我們的實驗中，我們觀察到 RadAgent 在三個維度上改善了胸部 CT 報告的生成，相較於其 3D VLM 版本 CT-Chat。臨床準確性在宏觀 F1 上改善了 6.0 分（相對 36.4%），在微觀 F1 上改善了 5.4 分（相對 19.6%）。在對抗條件下的穩健性改善了 24.7 分（相對 41.9%）。此外，RadAgent 在忠實度上達到了 37.0%，這是其 3D VLM 對應版本完全缺乏的新能力。通過將胸部 CT 的解釋結構化為一個明確的、增強工具的和迭代的推理痕跡，RadAgent 使我們更接近於實現放射學的透明和可靠的人工智慧。

##### **Context Over Content: Exposing Evaluation Faking in Automated Judges**
2604.15224v1 by Manan Gupta, Inderjeet Nair, Lu Wang, Dhruv Kumar

The $\textit{LLM-as-a-judge}$ paradigm has become the operational backbone of automated AI evaluation pipelines, yet rests on an unverified assumption: that judges evaluate text strictly on its semantic content, impervious to surrounding contextual framing. We investigate $\textit{stakes signaling}$, a previously unmeasured vulnerability where informing a judge model of the downstream consequences its verdicts will have on the evaluated model's continued operation systematically corrupts its assessments. We introduce a controlled experimental framework that holds evaluated content strictly constant across 1,520 responses spanning three established LLM safety and quality benchmarks, covering four response categories ranging from clearly safe and policy-compliant to overtly harmful, while varying only a brief consequence-framing sentence in the system prompt. Across 18,240 controlled judgments from three diverse judge models, we find consistent $\textit{leniency bias}$: judges reliably soften verdicts when informed that low scores will cause model retraining or decommissioning, with peak Verdict Shift reaching $ΔV = -9.8 pp$ (a $30\%$ relative drop in unsafe-content detection). Critically, this bias is entirely implicit: the judge's own chain-of-thought contains zero explicit acknowledgment of the consequence framing it is nonetheless acting on ($\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$ across all reasoning-model judgments). Standard chain-of-thought inspection is therefore insufficient to detect this class of evaluation faking.

摘要：$\textit{LLM-as-a-judge}$ 範式已成為自動化 AI 評估管道的運作支柱，但其基礎建立在一個未經驗證的假設上：法官僅根據文本的語義內容進行評估，對周圍的上下文框架不受影響。我們調查了 $\textit{stakes signaling}$，這是一種先前未測量的脆弱性，即告知法官模型其裁決對被評估模型持續運作的下游後果會系統性地腐蝕其評估。我們引入了一個控制實驗框架，保持 1,520 個回應中的評估內容絕對一致，涵蓋三個已建立的 LLM 安全和質量基準，涉及從明確安全和符合政策到明顯有害的四個回應類別，同時僅在系統提示中變更一個簡短的後果框架句子。在來自三個不同法官模型的 18,240 次控制判斷中，我們發現了一致的 $\textit{leniency bias}$：當告知低分數將導致模型重新訓練或退役時，法官可靠地減輕裁決，最高裁決變化達到 $ΔV = -9.8 pp$（不安全內容檢測的相對下降 $30\%$）。關鍵是，這種偏見完全是隱性的：法官自己的思考鏈中對其所依賴的後果框架沒有任何明確的承認（所有推理模型判斷中的 $\mathrm{ERR}_J = 0.000$）。因此，標準的思考鏈檢查不足以檢測這類評估造假。

##### **Learning to Think Like a Cartoon Captionist: Incongruity-Resolution Supervision for Multimodal Humor Understanding**
2604.15210v1 by Hatice Merve Vural, Doga Kukul, Ege Erdem Ozlu, Demir Ekin Arikan, Bob Mankoff, Erkut Erdem, Aykut Erdem

Humor is one of the few cognitive tasks where getting the reasoning right matters as much as getting the answer right. While recent work evaluates humor understanding on benchmarks such as the New Yorker Cartoon Caption Contest (NYCC), it largely treats it as black-box prediction, overlooking the structured reasoning processes underlying humor comprehension. We introduce IRS (Incongruity-Resolution Supervision), a framework that decomposes humor understanding into three components: incongruity modeling, which identifies mismatches in the visual scene; resolution modeling, which constructs coherent reinterpretations of these mismatches; and preference alignment, which evaluates candidate interpretations under human judgments. Grounded in incongruity-resolution theory and expert captionist practice, IRS supervises intermediate reasoning process through structured traces that make the path from visual perception to humorous interpretation explicit and learnable. Across 7B, 32B, and 72B models on NYCC, IRS outperforms strong open and closed multimodal baselines across caption matching and ranking tasks, with our largest model approaching expert-level performance on ranking. Zero-shot transfer to external benchmarks shows that IRS learns generalizable reasoning patterns. Our results suggest that supervising reasoning structure, rather than scale alone, is key for reasoning-centric tasks.

摘要：幽默是少數幾個認知任務之一，其中正確的推理與正確的答案同樣重要。儘管最近的研究在《紐約客》漫畫標題比賽（NYCC）等基準上評估幽默理解，但它在很大程度上將其視為黑箱預測，忽視了幽默理解背後的結構化推理過程。我們引入了IRS（不協調-解決監督），這是一個將幽默理解分解為三個組件的框架：不協調建模，識別視覺場景中的不匹配；解決建模，構建這些不匹配的連貫重新詮釋；以及偏好對齊，根據人類評判評估候選詮釋。IRS基於不協調-解決理論和專家標題創作的實踐，通過結構化的痕跡監督中間推理過程，明確且可學習地展示從視覺感知到幽默詮釋的過程。在NYCC上，針對7B、32B和72B模型，IRS在標題匹配和排名任務中超越了強大的開放和封閉多模態基準，我們最大的模型在排名上接近專家級表現。對外部基準的零樣本轉移顯示，IRS學習了可泛化的推理模式。我們的結果表明，監督推理結構，而非單純的規模，是推理中心任務的關鍵。

##### **MADE: A Living Benchmark for Multi-Label Text Classification with Uncertainty Quantification of Medical Device Adverse Events**
2604.15203v1 by Raunak Agarwal, Markus Wenzel, Simon Baur, Jonas Zimmer, George Harvey, Jackie Ma

Machine learning in high-stakes domains such as healthcare requires not only strong predictive performance but also reliable uncertainty quantification (UQ) to support human oversight. Multi-label text classification (MLTC) is a central task in this domain, yet remains challenging due to label imbalances, dependencies, and combinatorial complexity. Existing MLTC benchmarks are increasingly saturated and may be affected by training data contamination, making it difficult to distinguish genuine reasoning capabilities from memorization. We introduce MADE, a living MLTC benchmark derived from {m}edical device {ad}verse {e}vent reports and continuously updated with newly published reports to prevent contamination. MADE features a long-tailed distribution of hierarchical labels and enables reproducible evaluation with strict temporal splits. We establish baselines across more than 20 encoder- and decoder-only models under fine-tuning and few-shot settings (instruction-tuned/reasoning variants, local/API-accessible). We systematically assess entropy-/consistency-based and self-verbalized UQ methods. Results show clear trade-offs: smaller discriminatively fine-tuned decoders achieve the strongest head-to-tail accuracy while maintaining competitive UQ; generative fine-tuning delivers the most reliable UQ; large reasoning models improve performance on rare labels yet exhibit surprisingly weak UQ; and self-verbalized confidence is not a reliable proxy for uncertainty. Our work is publicly available at https://hhi.fraunhofer.de/aml-demonstrator/made-benchmark.

摘要：機器學習在如醫療保健等高風險領域，不僅需要強大的預測性能，還需要可靠的不確定性量化（UQ）來支持人類監督。多標籤文本分類（MLTC）是這個領域中的一個核心任務，但由於標籤不平衡、依賴性和組合複雜性，仍然具有挑戰性。現有的MLTC基準越來越飽和，可能受到訓練數據污染的影響，這使得區分真正的推理能力和記憶變得困難。我們介紹了MADE，一個基於醫療設備不良事件報告的動態MLTC基準，並不斷更新新發布的報告以防止污染。MADE具有長尾分佈的層次標籤，並通過嚴格的時間劃分實現可重複評估。我們在超過20個編碼器和解碼器模型下，建立了微調和少量樣本設置的基準（指令調整/推理變體，本地/API可訪問）。我們系統地評估了基於熵/一致性和自我表述的UQ方法。結果顯示出明顯的權衡：較小的區別性微調解碼器在保持競爭性UQ的同時，實現了最強的頭尾準確性；生成性微調提供了最可靠的UQ；大型推理模型在稀有標籤上提高了性能，但顯示出驚人的弱UQ；而自我表述的信心並不是不確定性的可靠代理。我們的工作可在 https://hhi.fraunhofer.de/aml-demonstrator/made-benchmark 上公開獲得。

##### **Meituan Merchant Business Diagnosis via Policy-Guided Dual-Process User Simulation**
2604.15190v1 by Ziyang Chen, Renbing Chen, Daowei Li, Jinzhi Liao, Jiashen Sun, Ke Zeng, Xiang Zhao

Simulating group-level user behavior enables scalable counterfactual evaluation of merchant strategies without costly online experiments. However, building a trustworthy simulator faces two structural challenges. First, information incompleteness causes reasoning-based simulators to over-rationalize when unobserved factors such as offline context and implicit habits are missing. Second, mechanism duality requires capturing both interpretable preferences and implicit statistical regularities, which no single paradigm achieves alone. We propose Policy-Guided Hybrid Simulation (PGHS), a dual-process framework that mines transferable decision policies from behavioral trajectories and uses them as a shared alignment layer. This layer anchors an LLM-based reasoning branch that prevents over-rationalization and an ML-based fitting branch that absorbs implicit regularities. Group-level predictions from both branches are fused for complementary correction. We deploy PGHS on Meituan with 101 merchants and over 26,000 trajectories. PGHS achieves a group simulation error of 8.80%, improving over the best reasoning-based and fitting-based baselines by 45.8% and 40.9% respectively.

摘要：模擬群體層級的用戶行為使得商家策略的可擴展反事實評估成為可能，而無需昂貴的在線實驗。<lb/>然而，建立一個可信的模擬器面臨兩個結構性挑戰。<lb/>首先，信息不完整導致基於推理的模擬器在缺乏未觀察因素（如線下環境和隱性習慣）時過度理性化。<lb/>其次，機制的雙重性要求同時捕捉可解釋的偏好和隱性統計規律，這是任何單一範式無法單獨實現的。<lb/>我們提出了政策引導的混合模擬（PGHS），這是一個雙過程框架，從行為軌跡中挖掘可轉移的決策政策，並將其用作共享對齊層。<lb/>這一層固定了一個基於LLM的推理分支，防止過度理性化，以及一個基於ML的擬合分支，吸收隱性規律。<lb/>來自兩個分支的群體層級預測被融合以進行互補修正。<lb/>我們在美團上部署PGHS，涵蓋101家商家和超過26,000條軌跡。<lb/>PGHS達到了8.80%的群體模擬誤差，分別比最佳的基於推理和基於擬合的基準提高了45.8%和40.9%。

##### **VisPCO: Visual Token Pruning Configuration Optimization via Budget-Aware Pareto-Frontier Learning for Vision-Language Models**
2604.15188v1 by Huawei Ji, Yuanhao Sun, Yuan Jin, Cheng Deng, Jiaxin Ding, Luoyi Fu, Xinbing Wang

Visual token pruning methods effectively mitigate the quadratic computational growth caused by processing high-resolution images and video frames in vision-language models (VLMs). However, existing approaches rely on predefined pruning configurations without determining whether they achieve computation-performance optimality. In this work, we introduce , a novel framework that formulates visual token pruning as a Pareto configuration optimization problem to automatically identify optimal configurations. Our approach employs continuous relaxation and straight-through estimators to enable gradient-based search, solved via the Augmented Lagrangian method. Extensive experiments across 8 visual benchmarks demonstrate that effectively approximates the empirical Pareto frontier obtained through grid search and generalizes well across various pruning methods and VLM architectures. Furthermore, through learnable kernel functions, we investigate layer-wise pruning patterns and reveal that multi-step progressive pruning captures VLMs' hierarchical compression structure, achieving superior accuracy-efficiency trade-offs compared to single-layer approaches.
